I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Management generator emits `new AbstractData()` for resources with discriminated (abstract) data types
## Problem

When a resource uses `DiscriminatedExtensionResource` (or any pattern that makes the resource data type abstract via `@discriminator`), the generated `Resource.Serialization.cs` creates a `DataDeserializationInstance` that tries to instantiate the abstract data type directly:

```csharp
// Generated in HciEdgeDeviceResource.Serialization.cs
private static IJsonModel<HciEdgeDeviceData> DataDeserializationInstance
    => s_dataDeserializationInstance ??= new Hci.HciEdgeDeviceData();
//                                       ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
//                                       CS0144: Cannot create an instance of the abstract type
```

Since `HciEdgeDeviceData` is abstract (generated from a `@discriminator`-decorated model), this produces **CS0144** at compile time.

## Affected Types (real-world example)

In the **Azure.ResourceManager.Hci** SDK (branch `migrate-hci-to-typespec`):

| Resource | Abstract Data Type | Error Location |
|---|---|---|
| `HciEdgeDeviceResource` | `HciEdgeDeviceData` | `HciEdgeDeviceResource.Serialization.cs:19` |
| `EdgeDeviceJobResource` | `EdgeDeviceJobData` | `EdgeDeviceJobResource.Serialization.cs:19` |

Both data types are abstract because their TypeSpec models use `DiscriminatedExtensionResource`:

```typespec
// EdgeDevice.tsp
@extensionResource
model EdgeDevice
  is Azure.ResourceManager.Legacy.DiscriminatedExtensionResource<DeviceKind> { ... }

// EdgeDeviceJob.tsp
@extensionResource
@parentResource(EdgeDevice)
model EdgeDeviceJob
  is Azure.ResourceManager.Legacy.DiscriminatedExtensionResource<EdgeDeviceKind> { ... }
```

## Minimal Repro

A minimal TypeSpec test file has been added to the mgmt test project at `eng/packages/http-client-csharp-mgmt/generator/TestProjects/Local/Mgmt-TypeSpec/discriminatedextensionresource.tsp`:

```typespec
@extensionResource
model PolyDevice
  is Azure.ResourceManager.Legacy.DiscriminatedExtensionResource<PolyDeviceKind> {
  ...ResourceNameParameter<
    Resource = PolyDevice,
    KeyName = "deviceName",
    SegmentName = "polyDevices",
    NamePattern = ""
  >;
}

union PolyDeviceKind {
  string,
  TypeA: "TypeA",
}

model TypeAPolyDevice extends PolyDevice {
  kind: PolyDeviceKind.TypeA;
  properties: TypeAPolyDeviceProperties;
}

model TypeAPolyDeviceProperties {
  description?: string;
}
```

## Expected Behavior

The generator should recognize that the resource data type is abstract and either:
1. Use a deserialization factory method that dispatches based on the discriminator property, or
2. Use one of the concrete derived types for the `DataDeserializationInstance`

Mgmt, CodeGen

    36	        internal static ResourceClientProvider Create(ArmResourceMetadata resourceMetadata, IReadOnlyList<ResourceMethod> methodsInResource, IReadOnlyList<ResourceMethod> methodsInCollection)
    37	        {
    38	            // Create a resource that supports multiple clients, using ResourceName from metadata
    39	            var resource = new ResourceClientProvider(resourceMetadata.ResourceName, resourceMetadata.ResourceModel, methodsInResource, resourceMetadata);
    40	            if (!resource.IsSingleton)
    41	            {
    42	                var collection = new ResourceCollectionClientProvider(resource, resourceMetadata.ResourceModel, methodsInCollection, resourceMetadata);
    43	                resource.ResourceCollection = collection;
    44	            }
    45	
    46	            return resource;
    47	        }

    68	            _inputModel = model;
    69	
    70	            _resourceTypeField = new FieldProvider(FieldModifiers.Public | FieldModifiers.Static | FieldModifiers.ReadOnly, typeof(ResourceType), "ResourceType", this, description: $"Gets the resource type for the operations.", initializationValue: Literal(ResourceTypeValue));
    71

    77

    79	            _clientInfos = resourceMetadata.CreateClientInfosMap(this);

   110	        private IReadOnlyList<ResourceClientProvider> BuildChildResources()
   111	        {
   112	            var childResources = new List<ResourceClientProvider>(_resourceMetadata.ChildResourceIds.Count);
   113	            // the resourcemetadata has a list of the ids of child resources
   114	            foreach (var childId in _resourceMetadata.ChildResourceIds)
   115	            {
   116	                // if the child resource id is not in the output library, we cannot find it.
   117	                var childResource = ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary.GetResourceById(childId);
   118	                if (childResource is null)
   119	                {
   120	                    ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.Emitter.ReportDiagnostic(
   121	                        "general-warning",
   122	                        $"Cannot find child resource with id {childId} for resource {ResourceName}."
   123	                    );
   124	                    continue;
   125	                }
   126	                childResources.Add(childResource);
   127	            }
   128	            return childResources;
   129	        }
   130	
   131	        private CSharpType BuildTypeOfParentResource()
   132	        {
   133	            if (_resourceMetadata.ResourceScope == ResourceScope.Extension)
   134	            {
   135	                return typeof(ArmResource);
   136	            }
   137	
   138	            // if the resource has a parent resource id, we can find it in the output library
   139	            if (_resourceMetadata.ParentResourceId is not null)
   140	            {
   141	                return ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary.GetResourceById(_resourceMetadata.ParentResourceId).Type;
   142	            }
   143	            // if it does not, this resource's parent must be one of the MockableResource
   144	            return ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.OutputLibrary.GetMockableResourceByScope(_resourceMetadata.ResourceScope).ArmCoreType;
   145	        }

   150	        private MethodSignature BuildFactoryMethodSignature()
   151	        {
   152	            if (ResourceCollection != null)
   153	            {
   154	                // we have the collection, we are not a singleton resource
   155	                var methodName = ResourceName.GetCollectionMethodName();
   156	                // Use inputIsKnownToBeSingular: false because some words like "Quota" and "Metadata"
   157	                // are treated by Humanizer as already plural (from Latin), and we want to preserve
   158	                // them unchanged rather than incorrectly pluralizing them.
   159	                var pluralOfResourceName = ResourceName.PluralizeLastWord(inputIsKnownToBeSingular: false);
   160	                return new MethodSignature(
   161	                    methodName,
   162	                    $"Gets a collection of {pluralOfResourceName} in the {TypeOfParentResource:C}",
   163	                    MethodSignatureModifiers.Public | MethodSignatureModifiers.Virtual,
   164	                    ResourceCollection.Type,
   165	                    $"An object representing collection of {pluralOfResourceName} and their operations over a {Name}.",
   166	                    [.. ResourceCollection.PathParameters]
   167	                    );
   168	            }
   169	            else
   170	            {
   171	                // we do not have a collection, we are a singleton resource
   172	                return new MethodSignature(
   173	                    $"Get{ResourceName}",
   174	                    $"Gets an object representing a {Type:C} along with the instance operations that can be performed on it in the {TypeOfParentResource:C}.",
   175	                    MethodSignatureModifiers.Public | MethodSignatureModifiers.Virtual,
   176	                    Type,
   177	                    $"Returns a {Type:C} object.",
   178	                    []
   179	                    );
   180	            }
   181	        }

   198	        {

   201	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public | MethodSignatureModifiers.Virtual,
   202	                typeof(bool),
   203	                "HasData",
   204	                new AutoPropertyBody(false),

   210	                ResourceData.Type,

   212	                new MethodPropertyBody(new MethodBodyStatement[]

   247	        private ConstructorProvider BuildResourceDataConstructor()
   248	        {
   249	            var clientParameter = new ParameterProvider("client", $"The client parameters to use in these operations.", typeof(ArmClient));
   250	            var dataParameter = new ParameterProvider("data", $"The resource that is the target of operations.", ResourceData.Type);
   251	
   252	            var initializer = new ConstructorInitializer(false, [clientParameter, dataParameter.Property("Id")]);
   253	            var signature = new ConstructorSignature(
   254	                Type,
   255	                $"Initializes a new instance of {Type:C} class.",
   256	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Internal,
   257	                [clientParameter, dataParameter],
   258	                null,
   259	                initializer);
   260	
   261	            var bodyStatements = new MethodBodyStatement[]
   262	            {
   263	                This.Property("HasData").Assign(Literal(true)).Terminate(),
   264	                _dataField.Assign(dataParameter).Terminate(),
   265	            };
   266	
   267	            return new ConstructorProvider(signature, bodyStatements, this);
   268	        }
   269	
   270	        private ConstructorProvider BuildResourceIdentifierConstructor()
   271	        {
   272	            var idParameter = new ParameterProvider("id", $"The identifier of the resource that is the target of operations.", typeof(ResourceIdentifier));
   273	            var parameters = new List<ParameterProvider>
   274	            {
   275	                new("client", $"The client parameters to use in these operations.", typeof(ArmClient)),
   276	                idParameter
   277	            };
   278	
   279	            var initializer = new ConstructorInitializer(true, parameters);
   280	            var signature = new ConstructorSignature(
   281	                Type,
   282	                $"Initializes a new instance of {Type:C} class.",
   283	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Internal,
   284	                parameters,
   285	                null,
   286	                initializer);
   287	
   288	            var thisResource = This.As<ArmResource>();
   289	
   290	            var bodyStatements = new List<MethodBodyStatement>();
   291	
   292	            bodyStatements.Add(thisResource.TryGetApiVersion(_resourceTypeField, $"{ResourceName}ApiVersion".ToVariableName(), out var apiVersion).Terminate());
   293	
   294	            // Initialize all client diagnostics and rest client fields
   295	            foreach (var (inputClient, clientInfo) in _clientInfos)
   296	            {
   297	                bodyStatements.Add(clientInfo.DiagnosticsField.Assign(New.Instance(typeof(ClientDiagnostics), Literal(Type.Namespace), _resourceTypeField.As<ResourceType>().Namespace(), thisResource.Diagnostics())).Terminate());
   298	                var effectiveApiVersion = apiVersion.NullCoalesce(Literal(inputClient.CurrentApiVersion));
   299	                bodyStatements.Add(clientInfo.RestClientField.Assign(New.Instance(clientInfo.RestClientProvider.Type, clientInfo.DiagnosticsField, thisResource.Pipeline(), thisResource.Endpoint(), effectiveApiVersion)).Terminate());
   300	            }
   301	
   302	            bodyStatements.Add(Static(Type).As<ArmResource>().ValidateResourceId(idParameter).Terminate());
   303	
   304	            return new ConstructorProvider(signature, bodyStatements.ToArray(), this);
   305	        }
   306	
   307	        private MethodProvider BuildCreateResourceIdentifierMethod()
   308	        {
   309	            var parameters = new List<ParameterProvider>();
   310	            var formatBuilder = new StringBuilder();
   311	            var refCount = 0;
   312	
   313	            foreach (var segment in _operationContext.ContextualPath)
   314	            {
   315	                if (segment.IsConstant)
   316	                {
   317	                    formatBuilder.Append($"/{segment}");
   318	                }
   319	                else
   320	                {
   321	                    if (formatBuilder.Length > 0)
   322	                    {
   323	                        formatBuilder.Append('/');
   324	                    }
   325	                    var variableName = segment.VariableName;
   326	                    var parameter = new ParameterProvider(variableName, $"The {variableName}", ResourceHelpers.GetRequestPathParameterType(variableName, _readMethod.InputMethod));
   327	                    parameters.Add(parameter);
   328	                    formatBuilder.Append($"{{{refCount++}}}");
   329	                }
   330	            }
   331	
   332	            var signature = new MethodSignature(
   333	                "CreateResourceIdentifier",
   334	                $"Generate the resource identifier for this resource.",
   335	                MethodSignatureModifiers.Public | MethodSignatureModifiers.Static,
   336	                typeof(ResourceIdentifier),
   337	                null,
   338	                parameters);
   339	
   340	            var bodyStatements = new MethodBodyStatement[]
   341	            {
   342	                Declare("resourceId", typeof(string), new FormattableStringExpression(formatBuilder.ToString(), parameters.Select(p => p.AsArgument()).ToArray()), out var resourceIdVar),
   343	                Return(New.Instance(typeof(ResourceIdentifier), resourceIdVar))
   344	            };
   345	
   346	            return new MethodProvider(signature, bodyStatements, this);
   347	        }
   348	
   349	        internal string ResourceTypeValue => _resourceMetadata.ResourceType;
   350	
   351	        protected override CSharpType? BuildBaseType() => typeof(ArmResource);
   352	
   353	        protected override MethodProvider[] BuildMethods()
   354	        {
   355	            var operationMethods = new List<MethodProvider>();
   356	            UpdateOperationMethodProvider? updateMethodProvider = null;
   357	
   358	            foreach (var resourceMethod in _resourceServiceMethods)
   359	            {
   360	                var methodKind = resourceMethod.Kind;
   361	                var method = resourceMethod.InputMethod;
   362	                var inputClient = resourceMethod.InputClient;
   363	
   364	                var isFakeLro = ResourceHelpers.ShouldMakeLro(methodKind);
   365	
   366	                // Get the appropriate rest client for this specific method
   367	                var restClientInfo = _clientInfos[inputClient];
   368	
   369	                var convenienceMethod = restClientInfo.RestClientProvider.GetConvenienceMethodByOperation(method.Operation, false);
   370	                var asyncConvenienceMethod = restClientInfo.RestClientProvider.GetConvenienceMethodByOperation(method.Operation, true);
   371	
   372	                if (method is InputPagingServiceMethod pagingMethod)
   373	                {
   374	                    // Use PageableOperationMethodProvider for InputPagingServiceMethod
   375	                    operationMethods.Add(new PageableOperationMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, restClientInfo, pagingMethod, true, methodName: ResourceHelpers.GetOperationMethodName(methodKind, true, false)));
   376	                    operationMethods.Add(new PageableOperationMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, restClientInfo, pagingMethod, false, methodName: ResourceHelpers.GetOperationMethodName(methodKind, false, false)));
   377	
   378	                    continue;
   379	                }
   380	
   381	                // Check if this is an update operation (PUT or Patch method for non-singleton resource)
   382	                var isUpdateOperation = (methodKind == ResourceOperationKind.Create || methodKind == ResourceOperationKind.Update) && !IsSingleton;
   383	
   384	                if (isUpdateOperation)
   385	                {
   386	                    var updateAsyncMethodProvider = new UpdateOperationMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, restClientInfo, method, true, methodKind, isFakeLro);
   387	                    operationMethods.Add(updateAsyncMethodProvider);
   388	
   389	                    updateMethodProvider = new UpdateOperationMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, restClientInfo, method, false, methodKind, isFakeLro);
   390	                    operationMethods.Add(updateMethodProvider);
   391	                }
   392	                else
   393	                {
   394	                    var asyncMethodName = ResourceHelpers.GetOperationMethodName(methodKind, true, false);
   395	                    operationMethods.Add(BuildResourceOperationMethod(method, restClientInfo, true, asyncMethodName, isFakeLro));
   396	                    var methodName = ResourceHelpers.GetOperationMethodName(methodKind, false, false);
   397	                    operationMethods.Add(BuildResourceOperationMethod(method, restClientInfo, false, methodName, isFakeLro));
   398	                }
   399	            }
   400	
   401	            var methods = new List<MethodProvider>
   402	            {
   403	                BuildCreateResourceIdentifierMethod(),
   404	                ResourceMethodSnippets.BuildValidateResourceIdMethod(this, _resourceTypeField)
   405	            };
   406	            methods.AddRange(operationMethods);
   407	
   408	            // Only generate tag methods if the resource model has tag properties, has get and update methods
   409	            if (HasTags() && _readMethod is not null)
   410	            {
   411	                (bool isPatch, ResourceMethod? tagUpdateMethod) = PopulateUpdateMethod();
   412	                if (tagUpdateMethod is not null)
   413	                {
   414	                    var inputReadMethod = _readMethod.InputMethod;
   415	                    var inputReadClient = _readMethod.InputClient;
   416	                    var inputUpdateClient = tagUpdateMethod.InputClient;
   417	                    if (inputReadClient is not null)
   418	                    {
   419	                        var updateRestClientInfo = _clientInfos[inputUpdateClient];
   420	                        var getRestClientInfo = _clientInfos[inputReadClient];
   421	                        var isFakeLro = ResourceHelpers.ShouldMakeLro(tagUpdateMethod.Kind);
   422	                        var tagUpdateMethodProvider = new UpdateOperationMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, updateRestClientInfo, tagUpdateMethod.InputMethod, false, tagUpdateMethod.Kind, isFakeLro);
   423	
   424	                        methods.AddRange([
   425	                            new AddTagMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, tagUpdateMethodProvider, inputReadMethod, updateRestClientInfo, getRestClientInfo, isPatch, true),
   426	                            new AddTagMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, tagUpdateMethodProvider, inputReadMethod, updateRestClientInfo, getRestClientInfo, isPatch, false),
   427	                            new SetTagsMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, tagUpdateMethodProvider, inputReadMethod, updateRestClientInfo, getRestClientInfo, isPatch, true),
   428	                            new SetTagsMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, tagUpdateMethodProvider, inputReadMethod, updateRestClientInfo, getRestClientInfo, isPatch, false),
   429	                            new RemoveTagMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, tagUpdateMethodProvider, inputReadMethod, updateRestClientInfo, getRestClientInfo, isPatch, true),
   430	                            new RemoveTagMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, tagUpdateMethodProvider, inputReadMethod, updateRestClientInfo, getRestClientInfo, isPatch, false)
   431	                        ]);
   432	                    }
   433	                }
   434	            }
   435	
   436	            // add method to get the child resource collection from the current resource.
   437	            methods.AddRange(BuildGetChildResourceMethods());
   438	
   439	            return [.. methods];
   440	        }
   441	
   442	        private MethodProvider BuildResourceOperationMethod(InputServiceMethod method, RestClientInfo restClientInfo, bool isAsync, string? methodName, bool isFakeLro)
   443	        {
   444	            // Check if the response body type is a list - if so, wrap it in a single-page pageable
   445	            var responseBodyType = method.GetResponseBodyType();
   446	            if (responseBodyType != null && responseBodyType.IsList)
   447	            {
   448	                return new ArrayResponseOperationMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, restClientInfo, method, isAsync, methodName);
   449	            }
   450	
   451	            return new ResourceOperationMethodProvider(this, _operationContext, restClientInfo, method, isAsync, methodName, forceLro: isFakeLro);
   452	        }
   453	
   454	        private (bool IsPatch, ResourceMethod? UpdateMethod) PopulateUpdateMethod()
   455	        {
   456	            // First try to find a patch method that has a body parameter whose model defines a tags property
   457	            // and returns content. A bodyless PATCH, one whose body model lacks tags, or one that returns
   458	            // no content cannot be used for tag operations — skip it.
   459	            var patchMethod = _resourceMetadata.Methods.FirstOrDefault(m => m.Kind == ResourceOperationKind.Update);
   460	            var patchBodyParameter = patchMethod?.InputMethod.Operation.Parameters.OfType<InputBodyParameter>().FirstOrDefault();
   461	            if (patchMethod is not null && patchBodyParameter is not null)
   462	            {
   463	                if (ModelHasTags(patchBodyParameter.Type as InputModelType) && OperationReturnsContent(patchMethod.InputMethod))
   464	                {
   465	                    return (true, patchMethod);
   466	                }
   467	
   468	                // PATCH has a body but either the body model does not define tags or the operation
   469	                // returns no content — do not fall back to PUT, as the resource intentionally omits
   470	                // tags from its update path.
   471	                return (false, null);
   472	            }
   473	
   474	            // If there is no patch method with a body, fall back to the put method
   475	            var putMethod = _resourceMetadata.Methods.FirstOrDefault(m => m.Kind == ResourceOperationKind.Create);
   476	            return (false, putMethod);
   477	        }
   478	
   479	        private static bool OperationReturnsContent(InputServiceMethod method)
   480	        {
   481	            if (method is InputLongRunningServiceMethod lroMethod)
   482	            {
   483	                return lroMethod.LongRunningServiceMetadata.ReturnType is not null;
   484	            }
   485	
   486	            var response = method.Operation.Responses.FirstOrDefault(r => !r.IsErrorResponse);
   487	            return response?.BodyType is not null;
   488	        }
   489	
   490	        private List<MethodProvider> BuildGetChildResourceMethods()
   491	        {
   492	            var methods = new List<MethodProvider>();
   493	
   494	            foreach (var childResource in ChildResources)
   495	            {
   496	                var thisResource = This.As<ArmResource>();
   497	                if (childResource.IsSingleton)
   498	                {
   499	                    var signature = childResource.FactoryMethodSignature;
   500	                    var lastSegment = childResource.ResourceTypeValue.Split('/')[^1];
   501	                    var bodyStatement = Return(New.Instance(childResource.Type, thisResource.Client(), thisResource.Id().AppendChildResource(Literal(lastSegment), Literal(childResource.SingletonResourceName!))));
   502	                    methods.Add(new MethodProvider(signature, bodyStatement, this));
   503	                }
   504	                else
   505	                {
   506	                    Debug.Assert(childResource.ResourceCollection is not null, "Child resource collection should not be null for non-singleton resources.");
   507	                    var signature = childResource.FactoryMethodSignature;
   508	                    MethodBodyStatement bodyStatement;
   509	                    if (signature.Parameters.Count > 0)
   510	                    {
   511	                        // When the collection getter has path parameters (e.g. nestedTypeName),
   512	                        // we must NOT use GetCachedClient because its cache key is only typeof(T),
   513	                        // which means different parameter values would return the same stale instance.
   514	                        bodyStatement = Return(New.Instance(childResource.ResourceCollection.Type,
   515	                            [thisResource.Client(), thisResource.Id(), .. signature.Parameters]));
   516	                    }
   517	                    else
   518	                    {
   519	                        bodyStatement = Return(thisResource.GetCachedClient(new CodeWriterDeclaration("client"),
   520	                            client => New.Instance(childResource.ResourceCollection.Type, client, thisResource.Id())));
   521	                    }
   522	                    methods.Add(new MethodProvider(signature, bodyStatement, this));
   523	                    // Add Get methods backed by collection's Get and GetAsync methods
   524	                    if (childResource.ResourceCollection.GetSyncMethodProvider is not null && childResource.ResourceCollection.GetAsyncMethodProvider is not null)
   525	                    {
   526	                        // Create both async and sync Get methods
   527	                        var methodProviders = new[]
   528	                        {
   529	                            (childResource.ResourceCollection.GetAsyncMethodProvider, true, "Async"),
   530	                            (childResource.ResourceCollection.GetSyncMethodProvider, false, "")
   531	                        };
   532	
   533	                        foreach (var (collectionMethodProvider, isAsync, suffix) in methodProviders)
   534	                        {
   535	                            var collectionSignature = collectionMethodProvider.Signature;
   536	                            var getMethodName = $"Get{childResource.ResourceName}{suffix}";
   537	
   538	                            var getSignature = new MethodSignature(
   539	                                getMethodName,
   540	                                collectionSignature.Description,
   541	                                collectionSignature.Modifiers,
   542	                                collectionSignature.ReturnType,
   543	                                collectionSignature.ReturnDescription,
   544	                                [.. signature.Parameters, .. collectionSignature.Parameters],
   545	                                [new AttributeStatement(typeof(ForwardsClientCallsAttribute))],
   546	                                collectionSignature.GenericArguments);
   547	
   548	                            var getBodyStatement = Return(
   549	                                thisResource.Invoke(signature.Name, signature.Parameters.Select(p => p.AsArgument()).ToArray())
   550	                                    .Invoke(collectionSignature.Name, collectionSignature.Parameters.Select(p => p.AsArgument()).ToArray(), null, isAsync));
   551	
   552	                            methods.Add(new MethodProvider(getSignature, getBodyStatement, this));
   553	                        }
   554	                    }
   555	                }
   556	            }
   557	
   558	            return methods;
   559	        }
   560	
   561	        private bool HasTags()
   562	        {
   563	            return ModelHasTags(_inputModel);
   564	        }
   565	
   566	        private static bool ModelHasTags(InputModelType? model)
   567	        {
   568	            InputModelType? currentModel = model;
   569	            while (currentModel != null)
   570	            {
   571	                foreach (var property in currentModel.Properties)
   572	                {
   573	                    if (property.SerializedName == "tags" && property.Type is InputDictionaryType
   574	                        {
   575	                            KeyType: InputPrimitiveType { Kind: InputPrimitiveTypeKind.String },
   576	                            ValueType: InputPrimitiveType { Kind: InputPrimitiveTypeKind.String }
   577	                        })
   578	                    {
   579	                        return true;
   580	                    }
   581	                }
   582	                currentModel = currentModel.BaseModel;
   583	            }
   584	            return false;
   585	        }
   586	    }
   587	}

    36	        /// <summary>
    37	        /// Indicates whether the ManagedServiceIdentityType enum uses v3 format
    38	        /// (no space in "SystemAssigned,UserAssigned"), which requires appending "|v3"
    39	        /// to the format for correct serialization of ManagedServiceIdentity.
    40	        /// </summary>
    41	        internal bool UseManagedServiceIdentityV3 => _useManagedServiceIdentityV3 ??= DetectManagedServiceIdentityV3();
    42	
    43	        private bool DetectManagedServiceIdentityV3()
    44	        {
    45	            var inputEnums = ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.InputLibrary.InputNamespace.Enums;
    46	            var identityTypeEnum = inputEnums.FirstOrDefault(e =>
    47	                e.CrossLanguageDefinitionId == "Azure.ResourceManager.CommonTypes.ManagedServiceIdentityType");
    48	            if (identityTypeEnum == null)
    49	                return false;
    50	            return identityTypeEnum.Values.Any(v =>
    51	                v.Value?.ToString() == "SystemAssigned,UserAssigned");

    54	        /// <summary>

    56	        /// For instance, if the namespace is "Azure.ResourceManager.Compute", the resource provider name will be "Compute".
    57	        /// </summary>

    59

    62	        /// Override this method to customize the prefix used for known type renaming.

    65	        {
    66	            const string armNamespacePrefix = "Azure.ResourceManager.";
    67	            if (PrimaryNamespace.StartsWith(armNamespacePrefix))
    68	            {
    69	                return PrimaryNamespace[armNamespacePrefix.Length..].ToIdentifierName();

    94	                    return inheritableType;

    97	                {
    98	                    return systemType;
    99	                }

   102	            if (inputType is InputEnumType enumType && KnownManagementTypes.TryGetSystemType(enumType.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var replacedType))
   103	            {
   104	                return replacedType;
   105	            }
   106	
   107	            if (inputType is InputPrimitiveType primitiveType && KnownManagementTypes.TryGetPrimitiveType(primitiveType.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var primitiveReplacedType))
   108	            {
   109	                return primitiveReplacedType;
   110	            }

   117	            // First check for standard ARM types that map to system types
   118	            if (KnownManagementTypes.TryGetInheritableSystemType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var replacedType))
   119	            {
   120	                return InheritableSystemObjectModelProvider.CreateSystemBase(replacedType.FrameworkType, model);
   121	            }
   122	            if (KnownManagementTypes.TryGetSystemType(model.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out _))
   123	            {
   124	                return null;
   125	            }
   126	
   127	            // For models whose base is an inheritable system type (e.g., TrackedResource → TrackedResourceData),
   128	            // use a derived InheritableSystemObjectModelProvider which overrides BuildBaseType() to return the
   129	            // correct framework CSharpType. The default ModelProvider.BuildBaseType() returns
   130	            // BaseModelProvider.Type, which produces a non-framework CSharpType that gets eagerly cached.
   131	            if (model.BaseModel is { } baseModel &&
   132	                KnownManagementTypes.TryGetInheritableSystemType(baseModel.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out var inheritableType))
   133	            {
   134	                CreateModel(baseModel);
   135	                return InheritableSystemObjectModelProvider.CreateDerived(model, inheritableType);
   136	            }
   137	
   138	            // For custom Azure resource models (root, intermediate, and resource data models),
   139	            // let the base implementation create regular ModelProviders.
   140	            // This preserves the full custom resource hierarchy without replacing intermediate
   141	            // models with system types (e.g., TrafficResource → TrafficProxyResource → TrafficEndpointData).
   142	            return base.CreateModelCore(model);
   143	        }
   144	
   145	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   146	        protected override EnumProvider? CreateEnumCore(InputEnumType enumType, TypeProvider? declaringType)
   147	        {
   148	            if (KnownManagementTypes.TryGetSystemType(enumType.CrossLanguageDefinitionId, out _))
   149	            {
   150	                return null;
   151	            }
   152	            return base.CreateEnumCore(enumType, declaringType);
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   156	        public override MethodBodyStatement SerializeJsonValue(CSharpType valueType, ValueExpression value, ScopedApi<Utf8JsonWriter> utf8JsonWriter, ScopedApi<ModelReaderWriterOptions> mrwOptionsParameter, SerializationFormat serializationFormat)
   157	        {
   158	            if (KnownManagementTypes.TryGetJsonSerializationExpression(valueType, out var serializationExpression))
   159	            {
   160	                return serializationExpression(valueType, value, utf8JsonWriter, mrwOptionsParameter, serializationFormat);
   161	            }
   162	
   163	            if (KnownManagementTypes.IsKnownManagementType(valueType))
   164	            {
   165	                // For ManagedServiceIdentity with v3 format, select pre-allocated v3 options
   166	                // based on the caller's format: WireV3Options for "W", JsonV3Options for "J".
   167	                // This preserves the base format semantics (principalId/tenantId included in "J").
   168	                ValueExpression optionsArg = valueType.AreNamesEqual(_managedServiceIdentityCSharpType) && UseManagedServiceIdentityV3
   169	                    ? new TernaryConditionalExpression(
   170	                        mrwOptionsParameter.Property("Format").Equal(Literal("W")),
   171	                        ModelSerializationExtensionsSnippets.WireV3,
   172	                        ModelSerializationExtensionsSnippets.JsonV3)
   173	                    : mrwOptionsParameter;
   174	                return value.CastTo(new CSharpType(typeof(IJsonModel<>), valueType)).Invoke(nameof(IJsonModel<object>.Write), [utf8JsonWriter, optionsArg]).Terminate();
   175	            }
   176	
   177	            return base.SerializeJsonValue(valueType, value, utf8JsonWriter, mrwOptionsParameter, serializationFormat);
   178	        }
   179	
   180	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   181	#pragma warning disable AZC0014 // Avoid using banned types in public API
   182	        public override ValueExpression DeserializeJsonValue(
   183	            CSharpType valueType,
   184	            ScopedApi<JsonElement> element,
   185	            ScopedApi<BinaryData> data,
   186	            ScopedApi<ModelReaderWriterOptions> mrwOptionsParameter,
   187	            SerializationFormat format)
   188	#pragma warning restore AZC0014 // Avoid using banned types in public API
   189	        {
   190	            if (KnownManagementTypes.TryGetJsonDeserializationExpression(valueType, out var deserializationExpression))
   191	            {
   192	                return deserializationExpression(valueType, element, format);
   193	            }
   194	
   195	            if (KnownManagementTypes.IsKnownManagementType(valueType))
   196	            {
   197	                // For ManagedServiceIdentity with v3 format, select pre-allocated v3 options
   198	                // based on the caller's format: WireV3Options for "W", JsonV3Options for "J".
   199	                ValueExpression wireOptions = valueType.AreNamesEqual(_managedServiceIdentityCSharpType) && UseManagedServiceIdentityV3
   200	                    ? new TernaryConditionalExpression(
   201	                        mrwOptionsParameter.Property("Format").Equal(Literal("W")),
   202	                        ModelSerializationExtensionsSnippets.WireV3,
   203	                        ModelSerializationExtensionsSnippets.JsonV3)
   204	                    : ModelSerializationExtensionsSnippets.Wire;
   205	
   206	                IReadOnlyList<ValueExpression> readBody =
   207	                [
   208	                    New.Instance(
   209	                    typeof(BinaryData),
   210	                    [
   211	                        new MemberExpression(typeof(Encoding), nameof(Encoding.UTF8)).Invoke(nameof(UTF8Encoding.GetBytes),
   212	                            [
   213	                                element.GetRawText()
   214	                            ])
   215	                    ]),
   216	                    wireOptions
   217	                ];
   218	
   219	                return Static(typeof(ModelReaderWriter)).Invoke(
   220	                    nameof(ModelReaderWriter.Read),
   221	                    [.. readBody, ModelReaderWriterContextSnippets.Default],
   222	                    typeArgs: [valueType]);
   223	            }
   224	
   225	            return base.DeserializeJsonValue(valueType, element, data, mrwOptionsParameter, format);
   226	        }
   227	
   228	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   229	        public override NewProjectScaffolding CreateNewProjectScaffolding()
   230	        {
   231	            return new NewManagementProjectScaffolding();
   232	        }
   233	    }
   234	}

- `HciEdgeDeviceData` is abstract (base class)
- `HciArcEnabledEdgeDevice` is a concrete derived type

Let me check if there's a newer version of the generator source vs the SDK output. Let me look at the `ResourceSerializationProvider.cs` again and trace what path would produce `UnknownEdgeDevice`:

The current code (line 44) is:
```csharp
new PropertyProvider(null, MethodSignatureModifiers.Private | MethodSignatureModifiers.Static, _jsonModelInterfaceType, "DataDeserializationInstance", new ExpressionPropertyBody(new AssignmentExpression(_dataField, New.Instance(_resourceDataType), true)), this)
```

This always creates `new <resourceDataType>()`. For the HCI SDK case, `_resourceDataType` would be `HciEdgeDeviceData` (which is abstract), so it would generate `new HciEdgeDeviceData()` which would fail.

But the generated file shows `new UnknownEdgeDevice()`. So either:
1. The generator was already fixed for the HCI SDK generation but the fix is not in `ResourceSerializationProvider.cs`
2. The HCI SDK code was manually fixed
3. There's a different code path

    87	        /// <summary>
    88	        /// This method initializes the resource clients, collections, and mockable clients.
    89	        /// We do all of these in the same method to ensure they are initialized together
    90	        /// </summary>
    91	        /// <param name="_resourcesByIdDict">Represent a map from resource id pattern to the <see cref="ResourceClientProvider"/>. </param>
    92	        /// <param name="_resources">The full list of <see cref="ResourceClientProvider"/>. </param>
    93	        /// <param name="_resourceCollections">The full list of <see cref="ResourceCollectionClientProvider"/>. </param>
    94	        /// <param name="_mockableResourcesByScopeDict">Represent a dictionary from scope to the corresponding <see cref="MockableResourceProvider"/>. </param>
    95	        /// <param name="_mockableResources">The full list of <see cref="MockableResourceProvider"/>. </param>
    96	        /// <param name="_extensionProvider">The <see cref="T:ExtensionProvider"/>. </param>
    97	        private static void InitializeResourceClients(
    98	            ref IReadOnlyDictionary<string, ResourceClientProvider>? _resourcesByIdDict,
    99	            ref IReadOnlyList<ResourceClientProvider>? _resources,
   100	            ref IReadOnlyList<ResourceCollectionClientProvider>? _resourceCollections,
   101	            ref IReadOnlyDictionary<ResourceScope, MockableResourceProvider>? _mockableResourcesByScopeDict,
   102	            ref IReadOnlyList<MockableResourceProvider>? _mockableResources,
   103	            ref ExtensionProvider? _extensionProvider)
   104	        {
   105	            if (_resourcesByIdDict is not null ||
   106	                _resources is not null ||
   107	                _resourceCollections is not null ||
   108	                _mockableResourcesByScopeDict is not null ||
   109	                _mockableResources is not null ||
   110	                _extensionProvider is not null)
   111	            {
   112	                return; // already initialized
   113	            }
   114	
   115	            var resourceMetadatas = ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.InputLibrary.ResourceMetadatas;
   116	            var resourceMethodCategories = new Dictionary<ArmResourceMetadata, ResourceMethodCategory>(resourceMetadatas.Count);
   117	
   118	            // build resource methods per resource metadata
   119	            var resourceDict = new Dictionary<ArmResourceMetadata, ResourceClientProvider>(resourceMetadatas.Count);
   120	            var collections = new List<ResourceCollectionClientProvider>(resourceMetadatas.Count);
   121	            foreach (var resourceMetadata in resourceMetadatas)
   122	            {
   123	                // categorize the resource methods
   124	                var categorizedMethods = resourceMetadata.CategorizeMethods();
   125	                // stores it because later in extensions we need it again
   126	                resourceMethodCategories.Add(resourceMetadata, categorizedMethods);
   127	                var resource = ResourceClientProvider.Create(resourceMetadata, categorizedMethods.MethodsInResource, categorizedMethods.MethodsInCollection);
   128	                resourceDict.Add(resourceMetadata, resource);
   129	                if (resource.ResourceCollection is not null)
   130	                {
   131	                    collections.Add(resource.ResourceCollection);
   132	                }
   133	            }
   134	
   135	            // resources and collections are now initialized
   136	            _resourcesByIdDict = resourceDict.ToDictionary(kv => kv.Key.ResourceIdPattern, kv => kv.Value);
   137	            _resources = [.. resourceDict.Values];
   138	            _resourceCollections = collections;
   139	
   140	            // build mockable resources
   141	            var resourcesAndMethodsPerScope = BuildResourcesAndNonResourceMethods(
   142	                resourceDict,
   143	                resourceMethodCategories,
   144	                ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.InputLibrary.NonResourceMethods);
   145	
   146	            // Extract extension non-resource methods for MockableArmClientProvider
   147	            var extensionNonResourceMethods = resourcesAndMethodsPerScope.TryGetValue(ResourceScope.Extension, out var extensionScope)
   148	                ? extensionScope.NonResourceMethods
   149	                : [];
   150	
   151	            var mockableArmClientResource = MockableArmClientProvider.TryCreate(_resources, extensionNonResourceMethods);
   152	            var mockableResources = new Dictionary<ResourceScope, MockableResourceProvider>(resourcesAndMethodsPerScope.Count);
   153	            foreach (var (scope, (resourcesInScope, resourceMethods, nonResourceMethods)) in resourcesAndMethodsPerScope)
   154	            {
   155	                if (scope != ResourceScope.Extension)
   156	                {
   157	                    var mockableExtension = MockableResourceProvider.TryCreate(scope, resourcesInScope, resourceMethods, nonResourceMethods);
   158	                    if (mockableExtension != null)
   159	                    {
   160	                        mockableResources.Add(scope, mockableExtension);
   161	                    }
   162	                }
   163	            }
   164	
   165	            _mockableResourcesByScopeDict = mockableResources;
   166	            var allMockableResources = new List<MockableResourceProvider>();
   167	            if (mockableArmClientResource != null)
   168	            {
   169	                allMockableResources.Add(mockableArmClientResource);
   170	            }
   171	            allMockableResources.AddRange(mockableResources.Values);
   172	            _mockableResources = allMockableResources;
   173	            _extensionProvider = new ExtensionProvider(_mockableResources);
   174	
   175	            static Dictionary<ResourceScope, ResourcesAndNonResourceMethodsInScope> BuildResourcesAndNonResourceMethods(
   176	                IReadOnlyDictionary<ArmResourceMetadata, ResourceClientProvider> resourceDict,
   177	                IReadOnlyDictionary<ArmResourceMetadata, ResourceMethodCategory> resourceMethods,
   178	                IEnumerable<NonResourceMethod> nonResourceMethods)
   179	            {
   180	                // walk through all resources to figure out their scopes
   181	                var resourcesAndMethodsPerScope = new Dictionary<ResourceScope, ResourcesAndNonResourceMethodsInScope>
   182	                {
   183	                    [ResourceScope.ResourceGroup] = new([], [], []),
   184	                    [ResourceScope.Subscription] = new([], [], []),
   185	                    [ResourceScope.Tenant] = new([], [], []),
   186	                    [ResourceScope.ManagementGroup] = new([], [], []),
   187	                    [ResourceScope.Extension] = new([], [], [])
   188	                };
   189	                foreach (var (metadata, resourceClient) in resourceDict)
   190	                {
   191	                    if (metadata.ParentResourceId is null)
   192	                    {
   193	                        resourcesAndMethodsPerScope[metadata.ResourceScope].ResourceClients.Add(resourceClient);
   194	                    }
   195	                }
   196	                foreach (var (metadata, category) in resourceMethods)
   197	                {
   198	                    // find the resource
   199	                    var resource = resourceDict[metadata];
   200	                    // the resource methods
   201	                    foreach (var resourceMethod in category.MethodsInExtension)
   202	                    {
   203	                        var resourcesAndMethodsInThisScope = resourcesAndMethodsPerScope[resourceMethod.OperationScope];
   204	                        if (!resourcesAndMethodsInThisScope.ResourceMethods.TryGetValue(resource, out var methods))
   205	                        {
   206	                            methods = new List<ResourceMethod>();
   207	                            resourcesAndMethodsInThisScope.ResourceMethods[resource] = methods;
   208	                        }
   209	                        // add this method into the list
   210	                        ((List<ResourceMethod>)methods).Add(resourceMethod);
   211	                    }
   212	                }
   213	                foreach (var nonResourceMethod in nonResourceMethods)
   214	                {
   215	                    resourcesAndMethodsPerScope[nonResourceMethod.OperationScope].NonResourceMethods.Add(nonResourceMethod);
   216	                }
   217	                return resourcesAndMethodsPerScope;
   218	            }
   219	        }

   242	
   243	        private void BuildModelTypes()
   244	        {
   245	            if (_modelFactoryModels is not null && _allModelTypes is not null)
   246	            {
   247	                return; // already built
   248	            }
   249	
   250	            var allModelTypes = new HashSet<CSharpType>();
   251	            var modelFactoryModels = new HashSet<CSharpType>();
   252	
   253	            foreach (var inputModel in ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.InputLibrary.InputNamespace.Models)
   254	            {
   255	                var model = ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateModel(inputModel);
   256	                if (model is not null)
   257	                {
   258	                    var eraseNullableType = model.Type.WithNullable(false);
   259	                    allModelTypes.Add(eraseNullableType);
   260	                    if (IsModelFactoryModel(model))
   261	                    {
   262	                        modelFactoryModels.Add(eraseNullableType);
   263	                    }
   264	                }
   265	            }
   266	
   267	            _allModelTypes = allModelTypes;
   268	            _modelFactoryModels = modelFactoryModels;
   269	        }
   270	
   271	        private static bool IsModelFactoryModel(ModelProvider model)
   272	        {
   273	            // A model is a model factory model if it is public and it has at least one public property without a setter.
   274	            return model.DeclarationModifiers.HasFlag(TypeSignatureModifiers.Public) && EnumerateAllPublicProperties(model).Any(prop => !prop.Body.HasSetter);
   275	
   276	            IEnumerable<PropertyProvider> EnumerateAllPublicProperties(ModelProvider current)
   277	            {
   278	                var currentModel = current;
   279	                foreach (var property in currentModel.Properties)
   280	                {
   281	                    if (property.Modifiers.HasFlag(MethodSignatureModifiers.Public))
   282	                    {
   283	                        yield return property;
   284	                    }
   285	                }
   286	
   287	                while (currentModel.BaseModelProvider is not null)
   288	                {
   289	                    currentModel = currentModel.BaseModelProvider;
   290	                    foreach (var property in currentModel.Properties)
   291	                    {
   292	                        if (property.Modifiers.HasFlag(MethodSignatureModifiers.Public))
   293	                        {
   294	                            yield return property;
   295	                        }
   296	                    }
   297	                }
   298	            }
   299	        }
   300	
   301	        internal bool IsModelFactoryModelType(CSharpType type) => ModelFactoryModels.Contains(type.WithNullable(false));
   302	
   303	        internal bool IsModelType(CSharpType type) => AllModelTypes.Contains(type.WithNullable(false));

   305	        /// <inheritdoc/>
   306	        protected override TypeProvider[] BuildTypeProviders()
   307	        {
   308	            // we need to add the clients (including resources, collections, mockable resources and extension static class)
   309	            // to the types to keep
   310	            // otherwise, they will be trimmed off or internalized by the post processor
   311	            foreach (var resource in ResourceProviders)
   312	            {
   313	                ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.AddTypeToKeep(resource.Name);
   314	            }
   315	            foreach (var collection in ResourceCollectionProviders)
   316	            {
   317	                ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.AddTypeToKeep(collection.Name);
   318	            }
   319	            foreach (var mockableResource in MockableResourceProviders)
   320	            {
   321	                ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.AddTypeToKeep(mockableResource.Name);
   322	            }
   323	            ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.AddTypeToKeep(ExtensionProvider.Name);
   324	
   325	            // Extract array response collection results from all methods
   326	            var arrayResponseCollectionResults = ExtractArrayResponseCollectionResults();
   327	
   328	            return [
   329	                .. base.BuildTypeProviders().Where(t => t is not InheritableSystemObjectModelProvider { IsSystemBase: true }),
   330	                WirePathAttributeDefinition,
   331	                ArmOperation,
   332	                ArmOperationOfT,
   333	                .. OperationSourceDict.Values,
   334	                ProviderConstants,
   335	                .. ResourceProviders,
   336	                .. ResourceCollectionProviders,
   337	                .. MockableResourceProviders,
   338	                ExtensionProvider,
   339	                PageableWrapper,
   340	                AsyncPageableWrapper,
   341	                .. arrayResponseCollectionResults,
   342	                .. ResourceProviders.SelectMany(r => r.SerializationProviders)];
   343	        }
   344	
   345	        private List<ArrayResponseCollectionResultDefinition> ExtractArrayResponseCollectionResults()
   346	        {
   347	            var collectionResults = new List<ArrayResponseCollectionResultDefinition>();
   348	
   349	            // Check all resource providers
   350	            foreach (var resource in ResourceProviders)
   351	            {
   352	                ExtractCollectionResultsFromMethods(resource.Methods, collectionResults);
   353	            }
   354	
   355	            // Check all resource collection providers
   356	            foreach (var collection in ResourceCollectionProviders)
   357	            {
   358	                ExtractCollectionResultsFromMethods(collection.Methods, collectionResults);
   359	            }
   360	
   361	            // Check all mockable resource providers
   362	            foreach (var mockableResource in MockableResourceProviders)
   363	            {
   364	                ExtractCollectionResultsFromMethods(mockableResource.Methods, collectionResults);
   365	            }
   366	
   367	            return collectionResults;
   368	        }
   369	
   370	        private void ExtractCollectionResultsFromMethods(IReadOnlyList<MethodProvider> methods, List<ArrayResponseCollectionResultDefinition> collectionResults)
   371	        {
   372	            foreach (var method in methods)
   373	            {
   374	                // Check if this is an ScmMethodProvider with an ArrayResponseCollectionResultDefinition
   375	                if (method is ScmMethodProvider { CollectionDefinition: ArrayResponseCollectionResultDefinition arrayCollectionResult })
   376	                {
   377	                    collectionResults.Add(arrayCollectionResult);
   378	                }
   379	            }
   380	        }
   381	
   382	        private Dictionary<CSharpType, OperationSourceProvider> BuildOperationSources()
   383	        {
   384	            var operationSources = new Dictionary<CSharpType, OperationSourceProvider>();
   385	
   386	            // Process resource methods
   387	            foreach (var metadata in ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.InputLibrary.ResourceMetadatas)
   388	            {
   389	                foreach (var resourceMethod in metadata.Methods)
   390	                {
   391	                    ProcessLroMethod(resourceMethod.InputMethod, operationSources);
   392	                }
   393	            }
   394	
   395	            // Process non-resource methods
   396	            foreach (var nonResourceMethod in ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.InputLibrary.NonResourceMethods)
   397	            {
   398	                ProcessLroMethod(nonResourceMethod.InputMethod, operationSources);
   399	            }
   400	
   401	            return operationSources;
   402	        }
   403	
   404	        private void ProcessLroMethod(InputServiceMethod inputMethod, Dictionary<CSharpType, OperationSourceProvider> operationSources)
   405	        {
   406	            if (inputMethod is InputLongRunningServiceMethod lroMethod)
   407	            {
   408	                var returnType = lroMethod.LongRunningServiceMetadata.ReturnType;
   409	                if (returnType is InputModelType inputModelType)
   410	                {
   411	                    var returnCSharpType = ManagementClientGenerator.Instance.TypeFactory.CreateCSharpType(inputModelType);
   412	                    if (returnCSharpType == null)
   413	                    {
   414	                        return;
   415	                    }
   416	
   417	                    // Find all resource providers that use this data type
   418	                    var resourceProviders = ResourceProviders.Where(r => r.ResourceData.Type.Equals(returnCSharpType));
   419	
   420	                    if (resourceProviders.Any())
   421	                    {
   422	                        // For each resource provider, create an OperationSource keyed by the resource type
   423	                        foreach (var resourceProvider in resourceProviders)
   424	                        {
   425	                            operationSources.TryAdd(resourceProvider.Type, new OperationSourceProvider(resourceProvider));
   426	                        }
   427	                    }
   428	                    else
   429	                    {
   430	                        // This is a non-resource model - use the data type as the key
   431	                        operationSources.TryAdd(returnCSharpType, new OperationSourceProvider(returnCSharpType));
   432	                    }
   433	                }
   434	            }
   435	        }
   436	
   437	        internal bool IsResourceModelType(CSharpType type) => GetResourceDataTypes().ContainsKey(type);
   438	
   439	        private IReadOnlyDictionary<CSharpType, List<ResourceClientProvider>>? _resourceDataTypes;
   440	        private IReadOnlyDictionary<CSharpType, List<ResourceClientProvider>> GetResourceDataTypes()
   441	        {
   442	            if (_resourceDataTypes == null)
   443	            {
   444	                var dict = new Dictionary<CSharpType, List<ResourceClientProvider>>();
   445	                foreach (var provider in ResourceProviders)
   446	                {
   447	                    if (!dict.TryGetValue(provider.ResourceData.Type, out var list))
   448	                    {
   449	                        list = new List<ResourceClientProvider>();
   450	                        dict[provider.ResourceData.Type] = list;
   451	                    }
   452	                    list.Add(provider);
   453	                }
   454	                _resourceDataTypes = dict;
   455	            }
   456	            return _resourceDataTypes;
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        internal bool TryGetResourceClientProvider(CSharpType resourceDataType, [MaybeNullWhen(false)] out ResourceClientProvider resourceClientProvider)
   460	        {
   461	            resourceClientProvider = null;
   462	            if (!GetResourceDataTypes().TryGetValue(resourceDataType, out var providers))
   463	            {
   464	                return false;
   465	            }
   466	
   467	            // Only wrap when the data type is exclusively used by one resource.
   468	            // When multiple resources share the same data type, wrapping would pick an arbitrary resource,
   469	            // so we skip wrapping and return the raw data type instead.
   470	            if (providers.Count != 1)
   471	            {
   472	                return false;
   473	            }
   474	
   475	            resourceClientProvider = providers[0];
   476	            return true;
   477	        }
   478	
   479	        private record ResourcesAndNonResourceMethodsInScope(
   480	            List<ResourceClientProvider> ResourceClients,
   481	            Dictionary<ResourceClientProvider, IReadOnlyList<ResourceMethod>> ResourceMethods,
   482	            List<NonResourceMethod> NonResourceMethods);
   483	    }
   484	}

2026-06-01 03:23:59,450 - INFO - swea-agent-Azure__azure-sdk-for-net-57616 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the issue. The fix needs to:

1. Store the `ModelProvider` (not just its `CSharpType`)
2. In `BuildProperties`, check if the model is abstract (has a discriminator)
3. If abstract, find the unknown discriminator model from `DerivedModels`
4. Use the unknown model's type for `New.Instance`

Let me also check how the existing generated HCI SDK code already got this right. Let me look at the `HciEdgeDeviceResource.Serialization.cs` again:

Line 17-18:
```csharp
private static UnknownEdgeDevice s_dataDeserializationInstance;
private static UnknownEdgeDevice DataDeserializationInstance => s_dataDeserializationInstance ??= new();
```

Note that the field type is `UnknownEdgeDevice` (the concrete type), not `IJsonModel<HciEdgeDeviceData>`. This is a different approach - they use the concrete type directly. But this works because `UnknownEdgeDevice` implements `IJsonModel<HciEdgeDeviceData>` through its base class.

However, the current generator code uses `IJsonModel<T>` as the field type. The approach I should take is:

1. If the resource data model is abstract, find the "unknown" derived model
2. Use the unknown model's type for `New.Instance()` 
3. Keep the field type as `IJsonModel<T>` (since the unknown model implements it)

Let me implement this:

    internal class ResourceSerializationProvider : TypeProvider
    {
        private readonly FieldProvider _dataField;
        private readonly CSharpType _resourceDataType;
        private readonly ResourceClientProvider _resoruce;
        private readonly CSharpType _jsonModelInterfaceType;
        private readonly ModelProvider _resourceDataModel;
        public ResourceSerializationProvider(ResourceClientProvider resource)
        {
            _resoruce = resource;
            _resourceDataModel = resource.ResourceData;
            _resourceDataType = resource.ResourceData.Type;
            _jsonModelInterfaceType = new CSharpType(typeof(IJsonModel<>), _resourceDataType);
            _dataField = new FieldProvider(FieldModifiers.Private | FieldModifiers.Static, _jsonModelInterfaceType, "s_dataDeserializationInstance", this);
        }

        protected override string BuildName() => _resoruce.Name;

        protected override string BuildRelativeFilePath()
            => Path.Combine("src", "Generated", $"{Name}.Serialization.cs");

        protected override PropertyProvider[] BuildProperties()
        {
            // Determine the type to instantiate for deserialization.
            // If the resource data model is abstract (has a discriminator), use the unknown variant.
            var instanceType = GetDeserializationInstanceType();
            return
            [
                new PropertyProvider(null, MethodSignatureModifiers.Private | MethodSignatureModifiers.Static, _jsonModelInterfaceType, "DataDeserializationInstance", new ExpressionPropertyBody(new AssignmentExpression(_dataField, New.Instance(instanceType), true)), this)
            ];
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets the type to use for deserialization instance.
        /// For discriminated (abstract) resource data models, returns the unknown discriminator model type;
        /// otherwise returns the resource data type itself.
        /// </summary>
        private CSharpType GetDeserializationInstanceType()
        {
            if (_resourceDataModel.DeclarationModifiers.HasFlag(TypeSignatureModifiers.Abstract))
            {
                var unknownModel = _resourceDataModel.DerivedModels.FirstOrDefault(m => m.IsUnknownDiscriminatorModel);
                if (unknownModel != null)
                {
                    return unknownModel.Type;
                }
            }
            return _resourceDataType;

// Copyright (c) Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.
// Licensed under the MIT License.

using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.ClientModel.Snippets;
using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Expressions;
using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Primitives;
using Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Providers;
using System;
using System.ClientModel.Primitives;
using System.IO;
using System.Linq;
using System.Text.Json;
using static Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Snippets.Snippet;

namespace Azure.Generator.Management.Providers
{
    internal class ResourceSerializationProvider : TypeProvider
    {
        private readonly FieldProvider _dataField;
        private readonly CSharpType _resourceDataType;
        private readonly ResourceClientProvider _resoruce;
        private readonly CSharpType _jsonModelInterfaceType;
        private readonly ModelProvider _resourceDataModel;
        public ResourceSerializationProvider(ResourceClientProvider resource)
        {
            _resoruce = resource;
            _resourceDataModel = resource.ResourceData;
            _resourceDataType = resource.ResourceData.Type;
            _jsonModelInterfaceType = new CSharpType(typeof(IJsonModel<>), _resourceDataType);
            _dataField = new FieldProvider(FieldModifiers.Private | FieldModifiers.Static, _jsonModelInterfaceType, "s_dataDeserializationInstance", this);
        }

        protected override string BuildName() => _resoruce.Name;

        protected override string BuildRelativeFilePath()
            => Path.Combine("src", "Generated", $"{Name}.Serialization.cs");

        protected override TypeSignatureModifiers BuildDeclarationModifiers()
            => TypeSignatureModifiers.Public | TypeSignatureModifiers.Partial;

        protected override CSharpType[] BuildImplements() => [_jsonModelInterfaceType];

        protected override FieldProvider[] BuildFields() => [_dataField];

        protected override PropertyProvider[] BuildProperties()
        {
            // Determine the type to instantiate for deserialization.
            // If the resource data model is abstract (has a discriminator), use the unknown variant.
            var instanceType = GetDeserializationInstanceType();
            return
            [
                new PropertyProvider(null, MethodSignatureModifiers.Private | MethodSignatureModifiers.Static, _jsonModelInterfaceType, "DataDeserializationInstance", new ExpressionPropertyBody(new AssignmentExpression(_dataField, New.Instance(instanceType), true)), this)
            ];
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Gets the type to use for deserialization instance.
        /// For discriminated (abstract) resource data models, returns the unknown discriminator model type;
        /// otherwise returns the resource data type itself.
        /// </summary>
        private CSharpType GetDeserializationInstanceType()
        {
            if (_resourceDataModel.DeclarationModifiers.HasFlag(TypeSignatureModifiers.Abstract))
            {
                var unknownModel = _resourceDataModel.DerivedModels.FirstOrDefault(m => m.IsUnknownDiscriminatorModel);
                if (unknownModel != null)
                {
                    return unknownModel.Type;
                }
            }
            return _resourceDataType;
        }

        protected override MethodProvider[] BuildMethods()
        {
            var options = new ParameterProvider("options", $"The client options for reading and writing models.", typeof(ModelReaderWriterOptions));
            var iModelTInterface = new CSharpType(typeof(IPersistableModel<>), _resourceDataType);
            var data = new ParameterProvider("data", $"The binary data to be processed.", typeof(BinaryData));

            // void IJsonModel<T>.Write(Utf8JsonWriter writer, ModelReaderWriterOptions options)
            var writer = new ParameterProvider("writer", $"The writer to serialize the model to.", typeof(Utf8JsonWriter));
            var jsonModelWriteMethod = new MethodProvider(
                new MethodSignature(nameof(IJsonModel<object>.Write), null, MethodSignatureModifiers.None, null, null, [writer, options], ExplicitInterface: _jsonModelInterfaceType),
                // => ((IJsonModel<T>)Data).Write(writer, options);
                new MemberExpression(null, "Data").CastTo(_jsonModelInterfaceType).Invoke(nameof(IJsonModel<object>.Write), writer, options),
                this);

            // T IJsonModel<T>.Create(ref Utf8JsonReader reader, ModelReaderWriterOptions options)
            var reader = new ParameterProvider("reader", $"The reader for deserializing the model.", typeof(Utf8JsonReader), isRef: true);
            var jsonModelCreatemethod = new MethodProvider(
                new MethodSignature(nameof(IJsonModel<object>.Create), null, MethodSignatureModifiers.None, _resourceDataType, null, [reader, options], ExplicitInterface: _jsonModelInterfaceType),
                // => DataDeserializationInstance.Create(reader, options);
                new MemberExpression(null, "DataDeserializationInstance").Invoke(nameof(IJsonModel<object>.Create), reader.AsArgument(), options),
                this);

            // BinaryData IPersistableModel<T>.Write(ModelReaderWriterOptions options)
            var persistableWriteMethod = new MethodProvider(
                new MethodSignature(nameof(IPersistableModel<object>.Write), null, MethodSignatureModifiers.None, typeof(BinaryData), null, [options], ExplicitInterface: iModelTInterface),
                // => ModelReaderWriter.Write<ResourceData>(Data, options);
                Static(typeof(ModelReaderWriter)).Invoke("Write", [new MemberExpression(null, "Data"), options, ModelReaderWriterContextSnippets.Default], [_resourceDataType], false),
                this);

            // T IPersistableModel<T>.Create(BinaryData data, ModelReaderWriterOptions options)
            var persistableCreateMethod = new MethodProvider(
                new MethodSignature(nameof(IPersistableModel<object>.Create), null, MethodSignatureModifiers.None, _resourceDataType, null, [data, options], ExplicitInterface: iModelTInterface),
                // => ModelReaderWriter.Read<ResourceData>(new BinaryData(reader.ValueSequence));
                Static(typeof(ModelReaderWriter)).Invoke("Read", [data, options, ModelReaderWriterContextSnippets.Default], [_resourceDataType], false),
                this);

            // ModelReaderWriterFormat IPersistableModel<T>.GetFormatFromOptions(ModelReaderWriterOptions options)
            var persistableGetFormatMethod = new MethodProvider(
                new MethodSignature(nameof(IPersistableModel<object>.GetFormatFromOptions), null, MethodSignatureModifiers.None, typeof(string), null, [options], ExplicitInterface: iModelTInterface),
                // => DataDeserializationInstance.GetFormatFromOptions(options);
                new MemberExpression(null, "DataDeserializationInstance").Invoke(nameof(IPersistableModel<object>.GetFormatFromOptions), options),
                this);

            return [jsonModelWriteMethod, jsonModelCreatemethod, persistableWriteMethod, persistableCreateMethod, persistableGetFormatMethod];
        }
    }
}
ENDOFFILE
