    17	    internal class PropertyHelpers
    18	    {
    19	        public static IReadOnlyList<PropertyProvider> GetAllProperties(ModelProvider propertyModelProvider)
    20	        {
    21	            var result = new List<PropertyProvider>();
    22	            var baseType = propertyModelProvider.BaseModelProvider;
    23	            var baseTypes = new Stack<ModelProvider>();
    24	
    25	            // Recursively get properties from base types
    26	            while (baseType is not null)
    27	            {
    28	                baseTypes.Push(baseType);
    29	                baseType = baseType.BaseModelProvider;
    30	            }
    31	            while (baseTypes.TryPop(out var item))
    32	            {
    33	                result.AddRange(item.Properties);
    34	                result.AddRange(item.CustomCodeView?.Properties ?? []);
    35	            }
    36	            result.AddRange(propertyModelProvider.Properties);
    37	            result.AddRange(propertyModelProvider.CustomCodeView?.Properties ?? []);
    38	            return result;
    39	        }
    40	
    41	        public static (bool IsReadOnly, bool? IncludeGetterNullCheck, bool IncludeSetterNullCheck) GetFlags(PropertyProvider property, PropertyProvider innerProperty)
    42	        {
    43	            var isInnerPropertyReadOnly = !innerProperty.Body.HasSetter;
    44	            var isPropertyReadOnly = !property.Body.HasSetter;
    45	            if (!isPropertyReadOnly && isInnerPropertyReadOnly)
    46	            {
    47	                if (HasDefaultPublicCtor(innerProperty.EnclosingType as ModelProvider))
    48	                {
    49	                    if (innerProperty.Type.Arguments.Count > 0)
    50	                        return (true, true, false);
    51	                    else
    52	                        return (true, false, false);
    53	                }
    54	                else
    55	                {
    56	                    return (false, false, false);
    57	                }
    58	            }
    59	            else if (!isPropertyReadOnly && !isInnerPropertyReadOnly)
    60	            {
    61	                if (HasDefaultPublicCtor(innerProperty.EnclosingType as ModelProvider))
    62	                    return (false, false, true);
    63	                else
    64	                    return (false, false, false);
    65	            }
    66	
    67	            return (true, null, false);
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        private static bool HasDefaultPublicCtor(ModelProvider? innerModel)
    71	        {
    72	            if (innerModel is null)
    73	                return false;
    74	
    75	            foreach (var ctor in innerModel.Constructors)
    76	            {
    77	                if (ctor.Signature.Modifiers.HasFlag(MethodSignatureModifiers.Public) && !ctor.Signature.Parameters.Any())
    78	                    return true;
    79	            }
    80	
    81	            return false;
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        public static MethodBodyStatement BuildGetter(bool? includeGetterNullCheck, PropertyProvider internalProperty, TypeProvider innerModel, PropertyProvider innerProperty)
    85	        {
    86	            var checkNullExpression = This.Property(internalProperty.Name).Is(Null);
    87	            // For collection types, we initialize the internal property if it's null and return the inner property.
    88	            if (innerProperty.Type.IsCollection && internalProperty.WireInfo?.IsRequired == true)
    89	            {
    90	                if (!internalProperty.Body.HasSetter)
    91	                {
    92	                    return Return(new TernaryConditionalExpression(checkNullExpression, Default, new MemberExpression(internalProperty, innerProperty.Name)));
    93	                }
    94	
    95	                return new List<MethodBodyStatement> {
    96	                    new IfStatement(checkNullExpression)
    97	                    {
    98	                        internalProperty.Assign(New.Instance(innerModel.Type)).Terminate()
    99	                    },
   100	                    Return(new MemberExpression(internalProperty, innerProperty.Name))
   101	                };
   102	            }
   103	
   104	            if (includeGetterNullCheck == true)
   105	            {
   106	                return new List<MethodBodyStatement> {
   107	                    new IfStatement(checkNullExpression)
   108	                    {
   109	                        internalProperty.Assign(New.Instance(innerModel.Type)).Terminate()
   110	                    },
   111	                    Return(new MemberExpression(internalProperty, innerProperty.Name))
   112	                };
   113	            }
   114	            else if (includeGetterNullCheck == false)
   115	            {
   116	                // For collection types with a settable internal property, initialize the internal property
   117	                // to avoid returning null, which would cause NullReferenceException during serialization.
   118	                if (innerProperty.Type.IsCollection && internalProperty.Body.HasSetter)
   119	                {
   120	                    return new List<MethodBodyStatement> {
   121	                        new IfStatement(checkNullExpression)
   122	                        {
   123	                            internalProperty.Assign(New.Instance(innerModel.Type)).Terminate()
   124	                        },
   125	                        Return(new MemberExpression(internalProperty, innerProperty.Name))
   126	                    };
   127	                }
   128	                return Return(new TernaryConditionalExpression(checkNullExpression, Default, new MemberExpression(internalProperty, innerProperty.Name)));
   129	            }
   130	            else
   131	            {
   132	                if (innerModel.Type.IsNullable)
   133	                {
   134	                    return Return(new MemberExpression(internalProperty.AsVariableExpression.NullConditional(), innerProperty.Name));
   135	                }
   136	                return Return(new MemberExpression(internalProperty, innerProperty.Name));
   137	            }
   138	        }
   139	
   140	        public static MethodBodyStatement? BuildSetterForPropertyFlatten(ModelProvider innerModel, PropertyProvider internalProperty, PropertyProvider innerProperty)
   141	        {
   142	            if (innerProperty.Type.IsCollection)
   143	            {
   144	                return null;
   145	            }
   146	
   147	            var isNullableValueType = innerProperty.Type.IsValueType && innerProperty.Type.IsNullable;
   148	            var setter = new List<MethodBodyStatement>();
   149	            var internalPropertyExpression = This.Property(internalProperty.Name);
   150	
   151	            setter.Add(
   152	                new IfStatement(internalPropertyExpression.Is(Null))
   153	                {
   154	                        internalPropertyExpression.Assign(New.Instance(innerModel.Type!)).Terminate()
   155	                });
   156	            setter.Add(internalPropertyExpression.Property(innerProperty.Name).Assign(isNullableValueType ? Value.Property(nameof(Nullable<int>.Value)) : Value).Terminate());
   157	            return setter;
   158	        }
   159	
   160	        public static MethodBodyStatement? BuildSetterForSafeFlatten(bool includeSetterCheck, ModelProvider innerModel, PropertyProvider internalProperty, PropertyProvider innerProperty)
   161	        {
   162	            // To not introduce breaking change, for collection types, we keep the setter for collection-type properties during safe flatten.
   163	            var isOverriddenValueType = IsOverriddenValueType(innerProperty);
   164	            var setter = new List<MethodBodyStatement>();
   165	            var internalPropertyExpression = This.Property(internalProperty.Name);
   166	            if (includeSetterCheck)
   167	            {
   168	                if (isOverriddenValueType)
   169	                {
   170	                    var ifStatement = new IfStatement(Value.Property(nameof(Nullable<int>.HasValue)))
   171	                    {
   172	                        new IfStatement(internalPropertyExpression.Is(Null))
   173	                        {
   174	                            internalPropertyExpression.Assign(New.Instance(innerModel.Type!)).Terminate(),
   175	                            internalPropertyExpression.Property(innerProperty.Name).Assign(Value.Property(nameof(Nullable<int>.Value))).Terminate()
   176	                        }
   177	                    };
   178	                    setter.Add(new IfElseStatement(ifStatement, internalProperty.AsVariableExpression.Assign(Null).Terminate()));
   179	                }
   180	                else
   181	                {
   182	                    setter.Add(new IfStatement(internalPropertyExpression.Is(Null))
   183	                    {
   184	                        internalPropertyExpression.Assign(New.Instance(innerModel.Type!)).Terminate()
   185	                    });
   186	                    setter.Add(internalPropertyExpression.Property(innerProperty.Name).Assign(Value).Terminate());
   187	                }
   188	            }
   189	            else
   190	            {
   191	                if (isOverriddenValueType)
   192	                {
   193	                    setter.Add(internalPropertyExpression.Assign(new TernaryConditionalExpression(Value.Property(nameof(Nullable<int>.HasValue)), New.Instance(innerModel.Type!, Value.Property(nameof(Nullable<int>.Value))), Default)).Terminate());
   194	                }
   195	                else
   196	                {
   197	                    setter.Add(internalPropertyExpression.Assign(New.Instance(innerModel.Type, Value)).Terminate());
   198	                }
   199	            }
   200	            return setter;
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        public static bool IsOverriddenValueType(PropertyProvider innerProperty)
   204	            => innerProperty.Type.IsValueType && !innerProperty.Type.IsNullable;
   205	
   206	        public static string GetCombinedPropertyName(PropertyProvider innerProperty, PropertyProvider immediateParentProperty)
   207	        {
   208	            var immediateParentPropertyName = GetPropertyName(immediateParentProperty);
   209	
   210	            if (innerProperty.Type.Equals(typeof(bool)) || innerProperty.Type.Equals(typeof(bool?)))
   211	            {
   212	                return innerProperty.Name.Equals("Enabled", StringComparison.Ordinal) ? $"{immediateParentPropertyName}{innerProperty.Name}" : innerProperty.Name;
   213	            }
   214	
   215	            if (innerProperty.Name.Equals("Id", StringComparison.Ordinal))
   216	                return $"{immediateParentPropertyName}{innerProperty.Name}";
   217	
   218	            if (immediateParentPropertyName.EndsWith(innerProperty.Name, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   219	                return immediateParentPropertyName;
   220	
   221	            var parentWords = immediateParentPropertyName.SplitByCamelCase();
   222	            bool suffixStripped = false;
   223	            if (immediateParentPropertyName.EndsWith("Profile", StringComparison.Ordinal) ||
   224	                immediateParentPropertyName.EndsWith("Policy", StringComparison.Ordinal) ||
   225	                immediateParentPropertyName.EndsWith("Configuration", StringComparison.Ordinal) ||
   226	                immediateParentPropertyName.EndsWith("Properties", StringComparison.Ordinal) ||
   227	                immediateParentPropertyName.EndsWith("Settings", StringComparison.Ordinal))
   228	            {
   229	                parentWords = parentWords.Take(parentWords.Count() - 1);
   230	                suffixStripped = true;
   231	            }
   232	
   233	            var parentWordArray = parentWords.ToArray();
   234	            var parentWordsHash = new HashSet<string>(parentWordArray);
   235	            var nameWords = innerProperty.Name.SplitByCamelCase().ToArray();
   236	            var lastWord = string.Empty;
   237	            for (int i = 0; i < nameWords.Length; i++)
   238	            {
   239	                var word = nameWords[i];
   240	                lastWord = word;
   241	                if (parentWordsHash.Contains(word))
   242	                {
   243	                    if (i == nameWords.Length - 2 && parentWordArray.Length >= 2 && word.Equals(parentWordArray[parentWordArray.Length - 2], StringComparison.Ordinal))
   244	                    {
   245	                        parentWords = parentWords.Take(parentWords.Count() - 2);
   246	                        break;
   247	                    }
   248	                    {
   249	                        return innerProperty.Name;
   250	                    }
   251	                }
   252	
   253	                //need to pluralize or singularize the last word and check
   254	                if (i == nameWords.Length - 1 && (parentWordsHash.Contains(lastWord.Pluralize()) || (suffixStripped && parentWordsHash.Contains(lastWord.Singularize()))))
   255	                    return innerProperty.Name;
   256	            }
   257	
   258	            immediateParentPropertyName = string.Join("", parentWords);
   259	
   260	            return $"{immediateParentPropertyName}{innerProperty.Name}";
   261	        }
   262	
   263	        private static string GetPropertyName(PropertyProvider property)
   264	        {
   265	            const string properties = "Properties";
   266	            if (property.Name.Equals(properties, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   267	            {
   268	                string typeName = property.Type.Name;
   269	                int index = typeName.IndexOf(properties);
   270	                if (index > -1 && index + properties.Length == typeName.Length)
   271	                    return typeName.Substring(0, index);
   272	
   273	                return typeName;
   274	            }
   275	            return property.Name;
   276	        }
   277	    }
   278	}

using System;
using System.Reflection;
using System.Linq;

var asm = Assembly.LoadFrom("/testbed/artifacts/bin/Azure.Generator.Management/Debug/net10.0/Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.dll");

// Check New.Instance signature
var snippetType = asm.GetType("Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Snippets.Snippet");
if (snippetType != null)
{
    foreach (var meth in snippetType.GetMethods(BindingFlags.Public | BindingFlags.Static | BindingFlags.DeclaredOnly))
    {
        if (meth.Name == "New" || meth.Name.StartsWith("New"))
        {
            Console.WriteLine($"  {meth.Name}({string.Join(", ", meth.GetParameters().Select(p => $"{p.ParameterType.Name} {p.Name}"))}) : {meth.ReturnType.Name}");
        }
    }
    
    // Also check for New.Instance
    var niType = asm.GetType("Microsoft.TypeSpec.Generator.Expressions.NewInstanceExpression");
    if (niType == null)
    {
        // maybe it's a nested type
        foreach (var t in asm.GetTypes())
        {
            if (t.Name.Contains("New"))
                Console.WriteLine($"  Type: {t.FullName}");
        }
    }
}

// Look for New expression
Console.WriteLine();
Console.WriteLine("=== Searching for New class ===");
foreach (var t in asm.GetTypes().Where(x => x.Name == "New" || x.Name == "Snippet"))
{
    Console.WriteLine($"Type: {t.FullName}");
    foreach (var meth in t.GetMethods(BindingFlags.Public | BindingFlags.Static))
    {
        if (meth.Name == "Instance")
        {
            foreach (var p in meth.GetParameters())
            {
                Console.WriteLine($"  param: {p.ParameterType.Name} {p.Name}");
            }
        }
    }
}

```csharp
internal UnknownEdgeDevice()
{
}
```

Yes, it has a parameterless constructor. And the base abstract class has `protected HciEdgeDeviceData()` which is also parameterless but protected.

My fix should work correctly.


- `internal UnknownEdgeDevice()` - internal, not public

- `protected HciEdgeDeviceData()` - protected
- `internal HciEdgeDeviceData(...)` - internal with parameters

And `UnknownEdgeDevice`:
- `internal UnknownEdgeDevice(...)` - internal with parameters (full constructor)
- `internal UnknownEdgeDevice()` - internal parameterless (for deserialization)

So the "unknown" model has a parameterless internal constructor. Good.

1. `_resourceDataModel` = `HciEdgeDeviceData` model provider
2. `_resourceDataModel.DeclarationModifiers` has `Abstract` flag

6. `New.Instance(unknownModel.Type)` generates `new UnknownEdgeDevice()`
